Coronavirus Deathtoll Visualized

Human Lives, Not A Statistic

By: Paul McBurney Jr | Inspired by neal.fun

543000 Deaths

544,000 is a big number. To put that massive number into perspective, let us visualize how other people die.

In comparison, in the 9/11 Terrorist Attacks the deathtoll is:

2,977 Deaths

To put that into perspective, every "emoji" below represents a live lost. As you scroll, think about the family, friends and aspirations they left behind.

To put that into perspective, every "emoji" below represents a live lost. Think of the family they left behind.

It's shocking to see every tiny "dot" representing a person with feelings, a family, and unfilfilled aspirations. Although this is extremely unfortunate, the best thing we can do is to put a stop to this virus' toll on human lives.
